<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разделять.html>разделя́ть</a> (4766)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разделить.html>раздели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razdelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разделять.html>разделя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razdeljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разделить.html>раздели́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to divide</li>
<li>to separate</li>
<li>to share (to have in common)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делить.html>дели́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">delítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разъединять.html>разъединя́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razʺjedinjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">расчленя́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rasčlenjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распределять.html>распределя́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raspredeljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***разделяться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разделяться.html>разделя́ться</a> (20411)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разделять.html>разделя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razdeljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разделяться.html>разделя́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razdeljátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разделиться.html>раздели́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to divide <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отряд.html>отря́д</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разделиться.html>раздели́лся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:четыре.html>четы́ре</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:группа.html>гру́ппы</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otrjád razdelílsja na četýre grúppy</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the detachment divided into four groups</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to separate, to part
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мнение.html>мне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разделиться.html>раздели́лись</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mnénija razdelílisʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">opinions were divided</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to divide</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разделять.html>разделя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razdeljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***раздеться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздеться.html>разде́ться</a> (6614)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздеть.html>разде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razdétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздеться.html>разде́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razdétʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздеваться.html>раздева́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to undress (oneself), to get undressed</li>

***раздирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздирать.html>раздира́ть</a> (12600)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-дира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-dirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздирать.html>раздира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razdirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разодрать.html>разодра́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tear up</li>
<li>to tear <i>(apart)</i>, to rend, to split
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раздирать.html>раздира́емый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:внутренний.html>вну́тренней</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:борьба.html>борьбо́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razdirájemyj</b> vnútrennej borʹbój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">torn by internal strife</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:война.html>войны</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раздирать.html>раздира́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:средневековый.html>средневеко́вую</a> Европу</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vojny <b>razdiráli</b> srednevekóvuju Jevropu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wars tore/rent medi(a)eval Europe</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раздирать.html>раздира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душу</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razdirátʹ</b> dušu/sérdce komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rend/lacerate/tear smb's heart</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***раздобыть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздобыть.html>раздобы́ть</a> (7269)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добыть.html>добы́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dobýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздобыть.html>раздобы́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razdobýtʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">раздобыва́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to procure, to get
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раздобыть.html>раздобы́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́нег</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razdobýtʹ</b> déneg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get (come by) some money</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***раздолбать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздолбать.html>раздолба́ть</a> (18347)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долбать.html>долба́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dolbátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздолбать.html>раздолба́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razdolbátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break using multiple blows</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to destroy by using sloppily</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to scold, to criticize</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздражаться.html>раздража́ться</a> (11785)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздражать.html>раздража́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razdražátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздражаться.html>раздража́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razdražátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">раздражи́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become irritated
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́жа</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раздражаться.html>раздража́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шерсть.html>ше́рсти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u menjá kóža <b>razdražájetsja</b> ot šérsti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wool irritates my skin</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to get irritated/annoyed, to chafe
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раздражаться.html>раздража́ться</a></b> и́з-за <a href = vnd.unilang:пустяк.html>пустяко́в</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пустяк.html>пустяка́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razdražátʹsja</b> íz-za pustjakóv/po pustjakám</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get irritated at a mere nothing</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напрасно.html>напра́сно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раздражаться.html>раздража́ется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">naprásno on <b>razdražájetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he shouldn't get so upset; there's nothing for him to be angry about</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздражать.html>раздража́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razdražátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздражить.html>раздражи́ть</a> (8430)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dražiti</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздражить.html>раздражи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razdražítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздражать.html>раздража́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to irritate</li>
<li>to annoy, to vex, to get on nerves</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздробить.html>раздроби́ть</a> (16634)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дробить.html>дроби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drobítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздробить.html>раздроби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razdrobítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дробить.html>дроби́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">раздробля́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to crush</li>
<li>to smash, to shatter</li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздроблённый.html>раздроблённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razdrobljónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздробить.html>раздроби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razdrobítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***раздувать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздувать.html>раздува́ть</a> (11295)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздуть.html>разду́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razdútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздувать.html>раздува́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razduvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздуть.html>разду́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fan, to blow</li>
<li>to inflate, to blow <i>(out)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раздувать.html>раздува́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razduvátʹ</b> ščóki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) to blow out one's cheeks; 2) to be puffed up; give oneself airs</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раздувать.html>раздува́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ноздря.html>но́здри</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razduvátʹ</b> nózdri</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dilate one's nostrils</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раздувать.html>раздува́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:парус.html>паруса́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">véter <b>razduvál</b> parusá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wind swelled out the sails</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to swell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздуть.html>разду́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёку</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó razdúlo licó (ščóku)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his face (cheek) is swollen</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blow up, to exaggerate</li>
<li>to fan, to boost
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раздувать.html>раздува́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:эмоция.html>эмо́ции</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razduvátʹ</b> emócii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fan emotions</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раздувать.html>раздува́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:короткий.html>коро́ткую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>речь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razduvátʹ</b> korótkuju rečʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pad a short speech</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раздувать.html>раздува́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:счет.html>счёт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:расход.html>расхо́дов</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razduvátʹ</b> sčót rasxódov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pad an expense account</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to blow about, to flutter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раздувать.html>раздува́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знамя.html>знамёна</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">véter <b>razduvájet</b> znamjóna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the colours/banners are flying/flapping in the wind</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***раздумать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздумать.html>разду́мать</a> (14111)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dúmatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздумать.html>разду́мать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razdúmatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздумывать.html>разду́мывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to change one's mind, to decide not
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раздумать.html>разду́мал</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:туда.html>туда́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>razdúmal</b> idtí tudá.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he has changed his mind about going there; he has decided not to go there</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
